class="noprint" id="mw-head-base"></div>\n<div class="mw-body" id="content" role="main">\n<a id="top"></a>\n<div class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice"><!-- CentralNotice --></div><div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n</div>\n<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of government space agencies</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"></div>\n<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>\n<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">"The Space Program" redirects here. For the song by A Tribe Called Quest, see <a href="/wiki/We_Got_It_from_Here..._Thank_You_4_Your_Service" title="We Got It from Here... Thank You 4 Your Service">We Got It from Here... Thank You 4 Your Service</a>.</div>\n<p>This is a list of <a href="/wiki/Government_agency" title="Government agency">government agencies</a> engaged in activities related to <a href="/wiki/Outer_space" title="Outer space">outer space</a> and <a href="/wiki/Space_exploration" title="Space exploration">space exploration</a>. (There is also a <a href="/wiki/List_of_private_spaceflight_companies" title="List of private spaceflight companies">List of private spaceflight companies</a>.)\n</p><p>As of 2018, 72 different government space agencies are in existence; 14 of those have launch capability. Six government space agencies&#8212;the <a href="/wiki/China_National_Space_Administration" title="China National Space Administration">China National Space Administration</a> (CNSA), the <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">European Space Agency</a> (ESA), the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indian_Space_Research_Organization" title="Indian Space Research Organization">Indian Space Research Organization</a> (ISRO), the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Japan_Aerospace_Exploration_Agency" title="Japan Aerospace Exploration Agency">Japan Aerospace Exploration Agency</a> (JAXA), the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Aeronautics_and_Space_Administration" title="National Aeronautics and Space Administration">National Aeronautics and Space Administration</a> (NASA), and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Federal_Space_Agency" title="Russian Federal Space Agency">Russian Federal Space Agency</a> (RFSA or Roscosmos)&#8212;have full launch capabilities; these include the ability to launch and recover multiple satellites, deploy cryogenic rocket engines and operate space probes. \n</p><p>The name given is the English version, with the native language version below. The acronym given is the most common acronym: this can either be the acronym of the English version (e.g. JAXA), or the acronym in the native language. Where there are multiple acronyms in common use, the English one is given first.\n</p><p>The date of the founding of the space agency is the date of first operations where applicable. If the space agency is no longer running, then the date when it was terminated (i.e. the last day of operations) is given. A link to the Agency\'s primary website is also given.\n</p>\n<div class="toc" id="toc"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div The budgets are not normalized to the expenses of space research in different countries, i.e. higher budget does not necessarily mean more activity or better performance in space exploration.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> Note also that budget could be used for different projects: e.g. GPS is maintained from the US defence budget, whereas ESA\'s money is used for developing the European Galileo positioning system. The data for authoritarian countries are unreliable. For European contributors to ESA, the national budgets shown include also their contributions to ESA.\n</p>\n<table cellpadding="1" class="BarChartTemplate" style="border-style:solid;
